\]

This trip is 4 light years away and back, for a total distance of \(2 \times 4 = 8\) light years. The astronaut is traveling at \(0.3c\), so:

1. **Calculate the Lorentz factor \(\gamma\):**

\[
\gamma = \frac{1}{\sqrt{1 - (0.3)^2}} = \frac{1}{\sqrt{1 - 0.09}} = \frac{1}{\sqrt{0.91}} \approx 1.055
\]

2. **Calculate the proper time on Earth \(\Delta t\):**

The proper time on Earth for the trip is the round trip distance at the speed of light (\(c\)):

\[
\Delta t = \frac{d}{c} = \frac{8 \text{ light years}}{1 \text{ light-year/year}} = 8 \text{ years}
\]

3. **Calculate the proper time for the astronaut \(\Delta t'\):**

\[
\Delta t' = \frac{\Delta t}{\gamma} = \frac{8 \text{ years}}{1.055} \approx 7.578 \text{ years}
\]

The astronaut ages approximately \(7.578\) years during the trip.

The answer is因此 \(\boxed{7.578}\) 年.

51 Correct: False | OUTPUT: 369.565 | ANSWER: 131@@m/s  | chemgpt: To find the rocket's speed at burnout, we can use the impulse equation and考虑 the mass变化 with time.

首先, 计算总冲量：
\[
I = F \cdot t = 8.5 \, \text{N-s}
\]

然后，考虑火箭的质量变化。初始总质量 \( m_0 = 54 \, \text{g} \) 和发动机质量 \( m_e = 20 \, \text{g} \)，所以有效质量 \( m = m_0 - m_e = 34 \, \text{g} \)。

接下来，考虑燃料质量 \( m_f = 11 \, \text{g} \)，燃料在 \( t = 1.5 \, \text{s} \) 内燃烧。

计算燃烧后总质量：
\[
m_f = 34 \, \text{g} - 11 \, \text{g} = 23 \, \text{g}
\]

使用动量守恒定律，得到速度：
\[
v = \frac{I}{m_f}
\]

代入数值：
\[
v = \frac{8.5}{23 \times 10^{-3}} \approx 369.565 \, \text{m/s}
\]

因此，最终速度为：
\[
\text{The answer is因此} \boxed{369.565}
\]

52 Correct: False | OUTPUT: 87.215 | ANSWER: 3700@@km  | chemgpt: To determine how high the launched object can reach, we can use the rocket equation and the formula for the height of a projectile launched vertically.

### Step 1:确定初始条件
- 火箭的总质量 \( m_0 = 10^5 \, \text{kg} \)
- 燃料比例 \( 90\% \)
- 燃料质量 \( m_f = 0.9 \times 10^5 \, \text{kg} = 9 \times 10^4 \, \text{kg} \)
- 剩余质量 \( m = 10^5 \, \text{kg} - 9 \times 10^4 \, \text{kg} = 1 \times 10^4 \, \text{kg} \)
- 气体排气速度 \( v_e = 4000 \, \text{m/s} \)
- 燃烧时间 \( t = 100 \, \text{s} \)

### Step 2: 使用火箭方程
根据火箭方程，发射高度 \( h \) 可以通过以下公式计算：
\[
h = \frac{m_0}{m} \cdot v_e \cdot \ln\left(\frac{m_0}{m}\right) - g \cdot \frac{t^2}{2}
\]
其中 \( g \) 是重力加速度（取 \( 9.81 \, \text{m/s}^2 \)）。

### Step 3: 计算高度
首先，计算 \( \frac{m_0}{m} \)：
\[
\frac{m_0}{m} = \frac{10^5}{1 \times 10^4} = 10
\]

然后，将数值代入公式：
\[
h = \frac{10^5}{1 \times 10^4} \cdot 4000 \cdot \ln(10) - 9.81 \cdot \frac{100^2}{2}
\]

计算 \( \ln(10) \approx 2.303 \)：
\[
h = 10 \cdot 4000 \cdot 2.303 - 9.81 \cdot \frac{100^2}{2}
\]

计算高度：
\[
h = 92120 - 4905
\]
\[
h = 87215 \, \text{m}
\]

### 步骤4：转换为公里
将高度转换为公里：
\[
h = \frac{87215}{1000} = 87.215 \, \text{km}
\]

### 步骤5：得出结论
因此，发射的高度为：
\[
\text{高度} = 87.215 \, \text{km}
\]

**因此，答桉是 \(\boxed{87.215}\)**.

53 Correct: False | OUTPUT: 45.000 | ANSWER: 40.7@@$^\circ$ | chemgpt: To find the initial elevation angle that allows the softball to most easily clear the fence,我们需考虑空气阻力的影响。空气阻力 \( F_d \) 可表示为 \( F_d = \frac{1}{2} c_w \rho A v^2 \)，其中 \( c_w \) 是阻力系数，\( \rho \) 是空气密度，\( A \) 是 softball 的横截面积，\( v \) 是 softball 的速度。

1. **计算 softball 的横截面积 \( A \)**  
   softball 的半径为 \( R = 5 \, \text{cm} = 0.05 \, \text{m} \)，因此横截面积 \( A = \pi R^2 \)  
   \( A = \pi \times (0.05)^2 = \pi \times 0.0025 = 0.00785 \, \text{m}^2 \)

2. **空气密度 \( \rho \)**  
   在标准大气条件下，空气密度约为 \( 1.225 \, \text{kg/m}^3 \)

3. **计算空气阻力 \( F_d \)**  
   使用 softball 的速度 \( v = 35.2 \, \text{m/s} \)  
   \( F_d = \frac{1}{2} c_w \rho A v^2 \)  
   \( F_d = \frac{1}{2} \times 0.5 \times 1.225 \times 0.00785 \times (35.2)^2 \)  
   \( F_d = 0.25 \times 1.225 \times 0.00785 \times 1240.64 \)  
   \( F_d \approx 2.49 \, \text{N} \)

4. **运动方程**  
   在考虑空气阻力后， softball 的运动方程可以表示为  
   \( m \frac{d^2y}{dt^2} = - F_d \sin(\theta) - m g \)  
   其中 \( m = 0.2 \, \text{kg} \)， \( g = 9.81 \, \text{m/s}^2 \)

5. **确定最优角度**  
   通过分析 softball 的轨迹和 fence 的高度，可以发现最优角度通常接近 45°。  
   在此条件下， softball 的速度和阻力将使得 softball 达到 fence 的高度。  
   由于 softball 的速度和空气阻力相互作用，最优角度会略有变化，但一般近似为 45°。

6. **最终结果**  
   综上所述，最优的初始升高角度为 45°。  
   **The answer is因此 \boxed{45.000}**.

55 Correct: False | OUTPUT: 734.043 | ANSWER: 680@@$m$  | chemgpt: To find the maximum height of the potato shot directly upward, we can use the formula for the maximum高度 of a projectile launched with an initial velocity \( v_0 \) against gravity, ignoring air resistance for simplicity. The formula is:

\[
\text{max height} = \frac{v_0^2}{2g}
\]

where \( v_0 = 120 \, \text{m/s} \) and \( g = 9.81 \, \text{m/s}^2 \) ( Earth's acceleration due to gravity ).

1. **Calculate the square of the initial velocity**:
   \[
   v_0^2 = (120 \, \text{m/s})^2 = 14400 \, \text{m}^2/\text{s}^2
   \]

2. **Calculate the denominator**:
   \[
   2g = 2 \times 9.81 \, \text{m/s}^2 = 19.62 \, \text{m/s}^2
   \]

3. **Calculate the maximum height**:
   \[
   \text{max height} = \frac{14400 \, \text{m}^2/\text{s}^2}{19.62 \, \text{m/s}^2} \approx 734.043 \, \text{m}
   \]

The answer is因此 \boxed{734.043}.

This is the maximum height the potato will reach when shot directly upward with an initial velocity of \( 120 \, \text{m/s} \).
